			exists = no
			any_unit_leader = {
				or = {
					has_trait = RUS_don_cossack
					has_trait = RUS_terek_cossack 
					has_trait = RUS_lineytsy_cossack
					has_trait = RUS_kuban_cossack

					has_trait = RUS_ural_cossack

# Absolutist Puppets

RUS_absolutist_great_game = {
RUS_ABSO_establish_rk_ROM = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 46
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROM = { exists = yes }
			}
			ROM = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
		46 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		OR = {
				46 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		ROM = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = ROM
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = ROM
				}
				remove_claim_by = ROM
			}
		}
		76 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		82 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		83 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		84 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		789 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		1112 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		1113 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		1114 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		1115 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		1116 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		1117 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		1118 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		79 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		81 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		713 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		46 = { add_core_of = ROM }
		release = ROM
		ROM = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = RUS
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = ROM
			}
		}
		ROM = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_ABSO_ROM_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "General-gubernator"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Imperial_Administration.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROM
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				authoritarian_democrat = 25
				paternal_autocrat = 50
				national_populist = 25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "General-gubernator"
				long_name = "General-gubernator"
			}
		}
	}
}

RUS_ABSO_establish_rk_IRQ = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 291
				state = 349
				state = 676
				state = 812
				state = 819
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				IRQ = { exists = yes }
			}
			IRQ = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
		291 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		349 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		676 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		812 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		819 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		OR = {
				291 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				349 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				676 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				812 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				819 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		IRQ = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = IRQ
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = IRQ
				}
				remove_claim_by = IRQ
			}
		}
		291 = { add_core_of = IRQ }
		349 = { add_core_of = IRQ }
		676 = { add_core_of = IRQ }
		812 = { add_core_of = IRQ }
		819 = { add_core_of = IRQ }
		release = IRQ
		IRQ = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = RUS
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = IRQ
			}
		}
		IRQ = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_ABSO_IRQ_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "General-gubernator"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Imperial_Administration.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = IRQ
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				authoritarian_democrat = 25
				paternal_autocrat = 50
				national_populist = 25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "General-gubernator"
				long_name = "General-gubernator"
			}
		}
	}
}

RUS_ABSO_establish_rk_TIB = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 322
				state = 693
				state = 748
				state = 1086
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				TIB = { exists = yes }
			}
			TIB = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
		322 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		693 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		748 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		1086 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		OR = {
				322 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				693 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				748 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				1086 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		TIB = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = TIB
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = TIB
				}
				remove_claim_by = TIB
			}
		}
		322 = { add_core_of = TIB }
		693 = { add_core_of = TIB }
		748 = { add_core_of = TIB }
		1086 = { add_core_of = TIB }
		release = TIB
		TIB = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = RUS
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = TIB
			}
		}
		TIB = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_ABSO_TIB_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "General-gubernator"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Imperial_Administration.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = TIB
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				authoritarian_democrat = 25
				paternal_autocrat = 50
				national_populist = 25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "General-gubernator"
				long_name = "General-gubernator"
			}
		}
	}

RUS_ABSO_establish_rk_INC = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 286
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { exists = yes }
			}
			INC = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
		286 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		OR = {
				286 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		INC = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = INC
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = INC
				}
				remove_claim_by = INC
			}
		}
		827 = { add_core_of = INC }
		670 = { add_core_of = INC }
		671 = { add_core_of = INC }
		826 = { add_core_of = INC }
		856 = { add_core_of = INC }
		857 = { add_core_of = INC }
		750 = { add_core_of = INC }
		825 = { add_core_of = INC }
		882 = { add_core_of = INC }
		286 = { add_core_of = INC }
		release = INC
		INC = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = RUS
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = INC
			}
		}
		INC = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_ABSO_INC_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "General-gubernator"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Imperial_Administration.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = INC
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				authoritarian_democrat = 25
				paternal_autocrat = 50
				national_populist = 25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "General-gubernator"
				long_name = "General-gubernator"

		}

	available = {
		if = {

				SWE = { exists = yes }
			}
			SWE = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
		38 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		124 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		138 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		139 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		140 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		141 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		666 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		778 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		908 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		909 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		960 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		OR = {
				38 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				124 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				138 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				139 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				140 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				141 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				666 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				778 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				908 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				909 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
				960 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		SWE = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = SWE
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = SWE
				}
				remove_claim_by = SWE
			}
		}
		38 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		124 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		138 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		139 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		140 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		141 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		666 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		778 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		908 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		909 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		960 = { add_core_of = SWE }
		release = SWE
		SWE = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = RUS
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = SWE
			}
		}
		SWE = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_CONST_SWE_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "General-gubernator"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Imperial_Administration.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = SWE
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				authoritarian_democrat = 25
				paternal_autocrat = 50
				national_populist = 25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "General-gubernator"
				long_name = "General-gubernator"
			}
		}
	}

RUS_CONST_establish_rk_PRU = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 303
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				PRU = { exists = yes }
			}
			PRU = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
		303 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		OR = {
				303 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		PRU = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = PRU
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = PRU
				}
				remove_claim_by = PRU
			}
		}
		490 = { add_core_of = PRU }
		872 = { add_core_of = PRU }
		491 = { add_core_of = PRU }
		492 = { add_core_of = PRU }
		494 = { add_core_of = PRU }
		845 = { add_core_of = PRU }
		303 = { add_core_of = PRU }
		release = PRU
		PRU = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = RUS
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = PRU
			}
		}
		PRU = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_CONST_PRU_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "General-gubernator"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Imperial_Administration.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PRU
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				authoritarian_democrat = 25
				paternal_autocrat = 50
				national_populist = 25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "General-gubernator"
				long_name = "General-gubernator"
			}
		}
	}
}
